$('.example-3-btn .tn-atom').attr('onclick', 'copytext3(".example-3-txt .tn-atom")');
function copytext3(el) {
var $tmp = $("<textarea>");
$("body").append($tmp);
$tmp.val($(el).text()).select();
document.execCommand("copy");
$tmp.remove();
